<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">internering</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></i>, likely a calque <a href = vnd.unilang:dating.html>dating</a> from the early days of the First World War.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:interneringskamp.html>interneringskamp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:interneringskampen.html>interneringskampen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An internment camp <span class="defdate">[from 1914]</span>.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>Likely borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">interplanétaire</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">interplanetary</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">inter-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:planetair.html>planetair</a></i>.
</p>

***interrumperen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:interrumperen.html>interrumperen</a> (128990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:interruptus.html>interruptus</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:interrumperen.html>interrumpere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to break apart, break to pieces, break off, interrupt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">inter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">between</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rumpere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:interrumperen.html>interrumperen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to interrupt</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:interrumperen.html>Interrumperen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used predominantly in politics; in everyday situations <i>in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rede.html>rede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:interrumperen.html>interrumperen</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:intocht.html>intocht</a> (69472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:intocht.html>intocht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:intocht.html>intochten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:intocht.html>intochtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:festivals.html>festivals</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> entry, entrance. Commonly used for the arrival of Sinterklaas in the country.</li>
<li>invasion
<ul><li><b>1947</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:anne.html>Anne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterhuis.html>Achterhuis</a></i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mei.html>Mei</a> 1940 <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bergaf.html>bergaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijden.html>tijden</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:capitulatie.html>capitulatie</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:intocht.html>intocht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Duitsers, <a href = vnd.unilang:waarna.html>waarna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ellende.html>ellende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:joden.html>Joden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begon.html>begon</a>.
<dl><dd>After May 1940, the good times <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> downhill: first the war, the capitulation, the German <b>invasion</b>, after which the misery for us Jews began.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inviteren.html>inviteren</a> (51602)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">inviter</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to invite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a modern borrowing (rather than descendant) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">invītāre</i>, present active infinitive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">invītō</i>.
</p>

***invoering.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:invoering.html>invoering</a> (49259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:invoeren.html>invoeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:invoering.html>invoering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>introduction (e.g. of a currency)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> 1945 <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:invoering.html>invoering</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijfje.html>vijfje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muntstuk.html>muntstuk</a> in 1988 <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> rijksdaalder <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogste.html>hoogste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarde.html>waarde</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rijksdaalder">[1]</a></sup> From 1945 until the introduction of the '<a href = vnd.unilang:fiver.html>fiver</a>' as coin in 1988, the rijksdaalder <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the coin with the highest value.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
